make(map[string]int)\n\t}\n\tm.calls[\"TransformToStorage\"]++\n\tif m.encryptErr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, m.encryptErr\n\t}\n\treturn m.encryptResult, nil\n}\n\nfunc (m *mockTransformer) TransformFromStorage(ctx context.Context, data []byte, dataCtx Context) ([]byte, bool, error) {\n\tif m.calls == nil {\n\t\tm.calls = make(map[string]int)\n\t}\n\tm.calls[\"TransformFromStorage\"]++\n\tif m.decryptErr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, false, m.decryptErr\n\t}\n\treturn m.decryptResult, m.stale, nil\n}\n\n//
